<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mississippi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="1334" height="255" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg/170px-Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg/255px-Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg/340px-Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi_Braves_Cody_Johnson.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mississippi Braves <a href="/wiki/Outfielder" title="Outfielder">outfielder</a> Cody Johnson at <a href="/wiki/Trustmark_Park" title="Trustmark Park">Trustmark Park</a></div></div></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_college_athletic_programs_in_Mississippi" title="List of college athletic programs in Mississippi">List of college athletic programs in Mississippi</a></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Biloxi,_Mississippi" title="Biloxi, Mississippi">Biloxi</a> is home to the <a href="/wiki/Biloxi_Shuckers" title="Biloxi Shuckers">Biloxi Shuckers</a> baseball team, a AA minor league affiliate of the <a href="/wiki/Milwaukee_Brewers" title="Milwaukee Brewers">Milwaukee Brewers</a> and member of the <a href="/wiki/Southern_League_(baseball)" title="Southern League (baseball)">Southern League</a> are currently located in Biloxi at <a href="/wiki/MGM_Park" title="MGM Park">MGM Park</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Clinton,_Mississippi" title="Clinton, Mississippi">Clinton</a> is home to the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Brilla" title="Mississippi Brilla">Mississippi Brilla</a> soccer team. The Brilla are a member of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USL_Premier_Development_League" title="USL Premier Development League">USL Premier Development League</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pearl,_Mississippi" title="Pearl, Mississippi">Pearl</a> is home to the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Braves" title="Mississippi Braves">Mississippi Braves</a> baseball team. The Braves are an AA minor league affiliate of the <a href="/wiki/Atlanta_Braves" title="Atlanta Braves">Atlanta Braves</a>. They play in the <a href="/wiki/Southern_League_(baseball)" title="Southern League (baseball)">Southern League</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_people">Notable people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mississippi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Notable people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_people_from_Mississippi" title="List of people from Mississippi">List of people from Mississippi</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="2448" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg/170px-Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg/255px-Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg/340px-Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Oprah_Winfrey_at_2011_TCA.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Oprah Winfrey, pictured in 2011, was born in <a href="/wiki/Kosciusko,_Mississippi" title="Kosciusko, Mississippi">Kosciusko</a>.</div></div></div>
<ul><li>Actors: <a href="/wiki/Lacey_Chabert" title="Lacey Chabert">Lacey Chabert</a>, <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Freeman" title="Morgan Freeman">Morgan Freeman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jim_Henson" title="Jim Henson">Jim Henson</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Earl_Jones" title="James Earl Jones">James Earl Jones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gerald_McRaney" title="Gerald McRaney">Gerald McRaney</a>, <a href="/wiki/Parker_Posey" title="Parker Posey">Parker Posey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Lynn_Spears" title="Jamie Lynn Spears">Jamie Lynn Spears</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sela_Ward" title="Sela Ward">Sela Ward</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Oprah_Winfrey" title="Oprah Winfrey">Oprah Winfrey</a></li>
<li>Artists: <a href="/wiki/Walter_Inglis_Anderson" title="Walter Inglis Anderson">Walter Inglis Anderson</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_E._Ohr" title="George E. Ohr">George E. Ohr</a></li>
<li>Athletes: <a href="/wiki/Leon_Bramlett" title="Leon Bramlett">Leon Bramlett</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ricky_Stenhouse,_Jr." title="Ricky Stenhouse, Jr.">Ricky Stenhouse, Jr.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cool_Papa_Bell" title="Cool Papa Bell">Cool Papa Bell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brett_Favre" title="Brett Favre">Brett Favre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kris_Mangum" title="Kris Mangum">Kris Mangum</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Mangum" title="John Mangum">John Mangum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Al_Jefferson" title="Al Jefferson">Al Jefferson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Monta_Ellis" title="Monta Ellis">Monta Ellis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clinton_Portis" title="Clinton Portis">Clinton Portis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Moulds" title="Eric Moulds">Eric Moulds</a>, <a href="/wiki/Archie_Manning" title="Archie Manning">Archie Manning</a>, <a href="/wiki/Deuce_McAllister" title="Deuce McAllister">Deuce McAllister</a>, <a href="/wiki/Steve_McNair" title="Steve McNair">Steve McNair</a>, <a href="/wiki/Travis_Outlaw" title="Travis Outlaw">Travis Outlaw</a>, <a href="/wiki/Walter_Payton" title="Walter Payton">Walter Payton</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jerry_Rice" title="Jerry Rice">Jerry Rice</a></li>
<li>Authors: <a href="/wiki/William_Faulkner" title="William Faulkner">William Faulkner</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Grisham" title="John Grisham">John Grisham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charlaine_Harris" title="Charlaine Harris">Charlaine Harris</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Harris" title="Thomas Harris">Thomas Harris</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany_Kent" title="Germany Kent">Germany Kent</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kathryn_Stockett" title="Kathryn Stockett">Kathryn Stockett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jesmyn_Ward" title="Jesmyn Ward">Jesmyn Ward</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eudora_Welty" title="Eudora Welty">Eudora Welty</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tennessee_Williams" title="Tennessee Williams">Tennessee Williams</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shelby_Foote" title="Shelby Foote">Shelby Foote</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barry_Hannah" title="Barry Hannah">Barry Hannah</a> and <a href="/wiki/Richard_Wright_(author)" title="Richard Wright (author)">Richard Wright</a></li>
<li>Civil rights leaders: <a href="/wiki/James_Bevel" title="James Bevel">James Bevel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Medgar_Evers" title="Medgar Evers">Medgar Evers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fannie_Lou_Hamer" title="Fannie Lou Hamer">Fannie Lou Hamer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Henry" title="Aaron Henry">Aaron Henry</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Meredith" title="James Meredith">James Meredith</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Anne_Moody" title="Anne Moody">Anne Moody</a></li>
<li>Classical musicians: <a href="/wiki/John_Alexander_(tenor)" title="John Alexander (tenor)">John Alexander</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ruby_Elzy" title="Ruby Elzy">Ruby Elzy</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Elizabeth_Taylor_Greenfield" title="Elizabeth Taylor Greenfield">Elizabeth Taylor Greenfield</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leontyne_Price" title="Leontyne Price">Leontyne Price</a>, and <a href="/wiki/William_Grant_Still" title="William Grant Still">William Grant Still</a></li>
<li>Fashion Designers: <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Kelly_(fashion_designer)" title="Patrick Kelly (fashion designer)">Patrick Kelly</a></li>
<li>Musicians: <a href="/wiki/Pepper_Keenan" title="Pepper Keenan">Pepper Keenan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jimi_Jamison" title="Jimi Jamison">Jimi Jamison</a>, <a href="/wiki/3_Doors_Down" title="3 Doors Down">3 Doors Down</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saving_Abel" title="Saving Abel">Saving Abel</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Banner" title="David Banner">David Banner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hayley_Williams" title="Hayley Williams">Hayley Williams</a>, <a href="/wiki/Big_K.R.I.T." title="Big K.R.I.T.">Big K.R.I.T.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lance_Bass" title="Lance Bass">Lance Bass</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brandy_(entertainer)" title="Brandy (entertainer)">Brandy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Buffett" title="Jimmy Buffett">Jimmy Buffett</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/David_L_Cook" title="David L Cook">David L Cook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bo_Diddley" title="Bo Diddley">Bo Diddley</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_%22Honeyboy%22_Edwards" title='David "Honeyboy" Edwards'>David "Honeyboy" Edwards</a>, <a href="/wiki/Faith_Hill" title="Faith Hill">Faith Hill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Randy_Houser" title="Randy Houser">Randy Houser</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_John_Hurt" title="Mississippi John Hurt">Mississippi John Hurt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Howlin%27_Wolf" title="Howlin' Wolf">Howlin' Wolf</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robert_Johnson_(musician)" title="Robert Johnson (musician)">Robert Johnson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albert_King" title="Albert King">Albert King</a>, <a href="/wiki/B.B._King" title="B.B. King">B.B. King</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denise_LaSalle" title="Denise LaSalle">Denise LaSalle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elvis_Presley" title="Elvis Presley">Elvis Presley</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charlie_Patton" title="Charlie Patton">Charlie Patton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charley_Pride" title="Charley Pride">Charley Pride</a>, <a href="/wiki/LeAnn_Rimes" title="LeAnn Rimes">LeAnn Rimes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jimmie_Rodgers_(country_singer)" title="Jimmie Rodgers (country singer)">Jimmie Rodgers</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Ruffin" title="David Ruffin">David Ruffin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Britney_Spears" title="Britney Spears">Britney Spears</a>, <a href="/wiki/Conway_Twitty" title="Conway Twitty">Conway Twitty</a>, <a href="/wiki/Muddy_Waters" title="Muddy Waters">Muddy Waters</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tammy_Wynette" title="Tammy Wynette">Tammy Wynette</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jumpin%27_Gene_Simmons" title="Jumpin' Gene Simmons">Jumpin' Gene Simmons</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bobbie_Gentry" title="Bobbie Gentry">Bobbie Gentry</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Blind_Melon" title="Blind Melon">Blind Melon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rick_Ross" title="Rick Ross">Rick Ross</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Soulja_Boy" title="Soulja Boy">Soulja Boy</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_culture">In popular culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mississippi&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: In popular culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="" data-file-height="40" data-file-width="40" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/40px-Ambox_important.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/60px-Ambox_important.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Ambox_important.svg/80px-Ambox_important.svg.png 2x" width="40"/></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This article <b>appears to contain <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:What_Wikipedia_is_not#Wikipedia_is_not_an_indiscriminate_collection_of_information" title="Wikipedia:What Wikipedia is not">trivial, minor, or unrelated</a> references to <a href='/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Trivia_sections#"In_popular_culture"_and_"Cultural_references"_material' title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Trivia sections">popular culture</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please reorganize this content to explain the subject's impact on popular culture, using <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">references</a> to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Identifying_reliable_sources" title="Wikipedia:Identifying reliable sources">reliable sources</a>, rather than simply listing appearances. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span> <small><i>(November 2017)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<ul><li>Children in the United States and Canada often count "One-Mississippi, two-Mississippi" during informal games such as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hide_and_seek" title="Hide and seek">hide and seek</a> to approximate counting by seconds.</li>
<li>Mississippi's low state rankings has given rise to the saying "<a href="/wiki/Thank_God_for_Mississippi" title="Thank God for Mississippi">Thank God for Mississippi</a>", denoting relief that the speaker's state isn't the lowest.</li>
<li>On March 12, 1894, the Biedenharn Candy Company bottled the first <a href="/wiki/Coca-Cola" title="Coca-Cola">Coca-Cola</a> in Vicksburg, Mississippi. <a href="/wiki/Root_beer" title="Root beer">Root beer</a> was invented in <a href="/wiki/Biloxi,_Mississippi" title="Biloxi, Mississippi">Biloxi</a> in 1898 by Edward Adolf Barq, the namesake of <a href="/wiki/Barq%27s" title="Barq's">Barq's Root Beer</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Teddy_bear" title="Teddy bear">Teddy bear</a> gets its name from President <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Roosevelt" title="Theodore Roosevelt">Theodore "Teddy" Roosevelt</a>. On a 1902 hunting trip to <a href="/wiki/Sharkey_County,_Mississippi" title="Sharkey County, Mississippi">Sharkey County, Mississippi</a>, he ordered the mercy killing of a wounded bear.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup></li>
<li>In 1935, the world's first night <a href="/wiki/Rodeo" title="Rodeo">rodeo</a> held outdoors under electric lights was produced by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Earl_Bascom" title="Earl Bascom">Earl Bascom</a> and Weldon Bascom in <a href="/wiki/Columbia,_Mississippi" title="Columbia, Mississippi">Columbia, Marion County, Mississippi</a></li>
<li>In 1936, <a href="/wiki/J._H._Rush" title="J. H. Rush">Dr. Leslie Rush</a>, of Rush Hospital in <a href="/wiki/Meridian,_Mississippi" title="Meridian, Mississippi">Meridian, Mississippi</a>, performed the first bone pinning in the United States. The "Rush Pin" is still in use.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Burnita_Shelton_Matthews" title="Burnita Shelton Matthews">Burnita Shelton Matthews</a> from near <a href="/wiki/Hazlehurst,_Mississippi" title="Hazlehurst, Mississippi">Hazlehurst, Mississippi</a>, was the first woman appointed as a judge of a <a href="/wiki/United_States_district_court" title="United States district court">U.S. district court</a>. She was appointed by <a href="/wiki/Harry_S._Truman" title="Harry S. Truman">Harry S. Truman</a> on October 21, 1949.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marilyn_Monroe" title="Marilyn Monroe">Marilyn Monroe</a> won the Mrs. Mississippi finals in the 1952 film <i><a href="/wiki/We%27re_Not_Married!" title="We're Not Married!">We're Not Married!</a></i>.</li>
<li>Texas Rose Bascom, of <a href="/wiki/Columbia,_Mississippi" title="Columbia, Mississippi">Columbia, Mississippi</a>, became the most famous female trick roper in the world, performing on stage and in Hollywood movies. She toured the world with <a href="/wiki/Bob_Hope" title="Bob Hope">Bob Hope</a>, billed as the "Queen of the Trick Ropers", and was the first Mississippian to be inducted into the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Cowgirl_Hall_of_Fame" title="National Cowgirl Hall of Fame">National Cowgirl Hall of Fame</a>.</li>
<li>In 1963, Dr. James D. Hardy of the University of Mississippi Medical Center performed the first human lung transplant in Jackson, Mississippi. In 1964, Dr. Hardy performed the first heart transplant, transplanting the heart of a chimpanzee into a human, where it beat for 90 minutes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup></li>
<li>"At 10:00 a.m. on October 22, 1964, the United States government detonated an underground nuclear device in Lamar County, in south Mississippi. (...) The <a href="/wiki/Salmon_Site" title="Salmon Site">Project Salmon</a> blast was about one-third as powerful as the bomb that destroyed Hiroshima in 1945. (...) The Project Sterling blast, on December 3, 1966, was considerably weaker than the blast two years earlier, as it was intended to be."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup></li>
<li>On January 8, 1935, <a href="/wiki/Elvis_Presley" title="Elvis Presley">Elvis Presley</a> was born in Tupelo.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup></li>
<li>In the 1964 song <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Goddam" title="Mississippi Goddam">Mississippi Goddam</a> the anger over racial murders in the southern states is described by <a href="/wiki/Nina_Simone" title="Nina Simone">Nina Simone</a>.</li>
<li>Several warships have been named <a href="/wiki/USS_Mississippi" title="USS Mississippi">USS <i>Mississippi</i></a>.</li>
<li>The comic book character <a href="/wiki/Rogue_(comics)" title="Rogue (comics)">Rogue</a>, from the well-known series <i><a href="/wiki/X-Men" title="X-Men">X-Men</a></i>, is a Mississippian and self-declared <a href="/wiki/Southern_belle" title="Southern belle">southern belle</a>. Her home town is located in the fictional county of Caldecott.</li>
<li>In 2013, researchers at the University of Mississippi Medical Center discovered a functional cure for <a href="/wiki/HIV/AIDS" title="HIV/AIDS">HIV/AIDS</a> in infants.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup></li>
<li>Many of legal thriller writer <a href="/wiki/John_Grisham" title="John Grisham">John Grisham</a>'s novels are set in and around the fictional town of Clanton, in the equally fictional Ford County, northwest Mississippi.</li>
<li>In <i>Star Trek</i>, Dr. Leonard "Bones" McCoy, Chief Medical Officer on the U.S.S. Enterprise, studied medicine at the University of Mississippi Medical Center.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Johnny_Carson" title="Johnny Carson">Johnny Carson</a> attended <a href="/wiki/Millsaps_College" title="Millsaps College">Millsaps College</a> under an elite Navy program to train officers, known as the <a href="/wiki/V-12_Navy_College_Training_Program" title="V-12 Navy College Training Program">V-12 Program</a> from November 1943 to February 1945.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></li>
<li>The film <i><a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Burning" title="Mississippi Burning">Mississippi Burning</a></i> (1988) is based around the FBI investigation of the 1964 <a href="/wiki/Murders_of_Chaney,_Goodman,_and_Schwerner" title="Murders of Chaney, Goodman, and Schwerner">murders of Chaney, Goodman, and Schwerner</a>. It stars Gene Hackman and Willem Dafoe.</li>
<li>The film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Help" title="The Help">The Help</a></i> (2011) was filmed on Grand Blv in Greenwood.</li></ul>
